SELECT `p`.`ProductId` AS `productId`, `p`.`Name` AS `name`, `p`.`Stock` AS `currentStock`, (

FROM (
    SELECT `o`.`OrderId`, `o`.`CreatedAt`, `o`.`OrderNumber`, `o`.`ShippingCost`, `o`.`Status`, `o`.`TotalAmount`, `o`.`UserId`, `s`.`ShippingId`, `s`.`City`, `s`.`CityRef`, `s`.`OrderId` AS `OrderId0`, `s`.`RecipientName`, `s`.`RecipientPhone`, `s`.`TrackingNumber`, `s`.`WarehouseNumber`, `s`.`WarehouseRef`, `p`.`PaymentId`, `p`.`Amount`, `p`.`CreatedAt` AS `CreatedAt0`, `p`.`IdempotencyKey`, `p`.`Method`, `p`.`OrderId` AS `OrderId1`, `p`.`Status` AS `Status0`, `p`.`StripePaymentIntentId`, `p`.`StripeSessionId`, `p`.`TransactionId`, `p`.`UpdatedAt`

    LEFT JOIN `productimages` AS `p0` ON `p`.`ProductId` = `p0`.`ProductId`
) AS `t0` ON `t`.`CartId` = `t0`.`CartId`
ORDER BY `t`.`CartId`, `t0`.`CartItemId`, `t0`.`ProductId0`, `t0`.`CategoryId0`
